25:T5017,<entryFree id="n346" key="أخَذَ" type="main">     
                  <form>       
                     <itype>1</itype>        
                     <orth orig="" extent="full" lang="ar">أخَذَ</orth>
                     <orth extent="full" lang="ar">ذ</orth>
                  </form>, (S, A, L, &amp;c.,) in the first pers. of which, <foreign lang="ar">أَخَذْتُ</foreign>, [and the like,] the <foreign lang="ar">ذ</foreign> is generally changed into <foreign lang="ar">ت</foreign>, and incorporated into the [augmentative] <foreign lang="ar">ت</foreign>, [but in pronunciation only, for one writes <foreign lang="ar">أَخَذتُّ</foreign> and the like,] aor.      
    <form n="infl">       
                     <orth orig="Bu" lang="ar">اَخُذَ</orth>
                  </form>, imperative <foreign lang="ar">خُذْ</foreign>, originally <foreign lang="ar">ٱؤْخُذْ</foreign>, (S, L,) which latter form sometimes occurs, [but with <foreign lang="ar">و</foreign> in the place of <foreign lang="ar">ؤْ</foreign> when the <foreign lang="ar">ا</foreign> is pronounced with damm,] (TA,) inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">أَخْذٌ</foreign> (S, L, Msb, K, &amp;c.) and <foreign lang="ar">تَأْخَاذٌ</foreign>, (S, L, K,) the latter having an intensive signification; (MF;) and <foreign lang="ar">وَخَذَ</foreign> is a dial. var., as mentioned by Ibn-Umm-Kásim and others on the authority of AHei; (MF in art. <foreign lang="ar">تخذ</foreign>;) <hi rend="ital">He took; he took with his hand; he took hold of;</hi> (S, A, L, Msb, K;) a thing. (S, L.) You say, <foreign lang="ar">خُذِ الخِطَامَ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">خُذْ بِالخِطَامَ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">Take thou,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">take thou with thy hand,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">take thou hold of, the nose-rein</hi> of the camel: (S, L, Msb:) the <foreign lang="ar">ب</foreign> in the latter phrase being redundant. (Msb.) [And <foreign lang="ar">أَخَذَ بِيَدِهِ</foreign>, lit. <hi rend="ital">He took his hand,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">arm;</hi> meaning <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  <hi rend="ital">he aided,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">assisted, him:</hi> a phrase of frequent occurrence.] And <foreign lang="ar">أَخَذَ عَلَىيَدِ فُلَانٍ</foreign> <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  <hi rend="ital">He prevented, restrained,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">withheld, such a one from doing that which he desired; as though he laid hold upon his hand,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">arm:</hi> (L:) and <foreign lang="ar">أَخَذَ عَلَى يَدِهِ دُونَ مَا يُرِيُدهُ</foreign> [signifies the same]. (K in art. <foreign lang="ar">لغد</foreign>.)          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  Also, inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">أَخْذٌ</foreign>, <hi rend="ital">He took,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">received; contr. of</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">أَعْطَي</foreign>. (L.) [Hence,] <foreign lang="ar">أَخَذَ عَنْهُ</foreign>, <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  <hi rend="ital">He received from him traditions,</hi> and <hi rend="ital">the like.</hi> (TA passim.)          <sense type="b" n="3">-b3-</sense>  <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  [<hi rend="ital">He took,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">derived,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">deduced,</hi> a word, a phrase, and a meaning.]          <sense type="b" n="4">-b4-</sense>  <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  <hi rend="ital">He took, received,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">admitted, willingly,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">with approbation; he accepted.</hi> (B, MF.) So in the Kur [vii. 198], <foreign lang="ar">خُذِ العَفْوَ</foreign> <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  [<hi rend="ital">Take thou willingly,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">accept thou, superfluous property,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">such as is easily spared</hi> by others]. (MF.) So too in the same [iii. 75], <foreign lang="ar">وَ أَخَذتُّمْ عَلَي ذٰلِكُمْ إِصْرِى</foreign> <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  [<hi rend="ital">And do ye accept my covenant to that effect?</hi>]. (B.) [And in the phrases, <foreign lang="ar">أَخَذْنَا مِيثَاقَكُمْ بِالعَمَلِ بِمَا فِي التَّوْارَاةِ</foreign>, (Jel ii. 60,) and <foreign lang="ar">عَلَي العَمّلِ بما في التوارة</foreign>, (Idem ii. 87,) <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  <hi rend="ital">We accepted your covenant to do according to what is in the Book of the Law revealed to Moses.</hi>] <foreign lang="ar">خُذْ عَنْكَ</foreign> [is elliptical, and] means <foreign lang="ar">خُذْ مَا أَقُولُ وَدَع عَنْكَ الشَّكَ والمِرآءَ</foreign> <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  [<hi rend="ital">Accept thou what I say, and dismiss from thee doubt and obstinate disputation</hi>]. (S, L.)          <sense type="b" n="5">-b5-</sense>  <hi rend="ital">He took</hi> a thing <hi rend="ital">to,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">for, himself; took possession of</hi> it; <hi rend="ital">got,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">acquired,</hi> it; syn. <foreign lang="ar">حَازَ</foreign>; (Z, Er-Rághib, B;) which, accord. to Z and Er-Rághib and others, is the primary signification; (MF;) and <foreign lang="ar">حَصَّلَ</foreign>. (B.) [See also 8.]          <sense type="b" n="6">-b6-</sense>  [<hi rend="ital">He took and kept;</hi>] <hi rend="ital">he retained; he detained:</hi> as in the Kur [xii. 78], <foreign lang="ar">فَخُذْ أَحَدَنَا مَكَانَهُ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">Therefore retain thou one of us in his stead</hi>]. (B.)          <sense type="b" n="7">-b7-</sense>  [<hi rend="ital">He took,</hi> as meaning <hi rend="ital">he took away.</hi> Hence,] <foreign lang="ar">أَخَذَ مِنْهُ السَّيْرُ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">Journeying,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">travel, took from him strength;</hi> (<foreign lang="ar">القُوَّةَ</foreign> being understood;) <hi rend="ital">weakened him.</hi> (Har p. 529.) And <foreign lang="ar">أَخَذَ مِنَ الشَّارِبِ</foreign>, (Mgh,) and <foreign lang="ar">مِنَ الشَّعَرِ</foreign>, (Msb,) <hi rend="ital">He clipped,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">cut off from,</hi> (Mgh, Msb,) <hi rend="ital">the mustache,</hi> (Mgh,) and <hi rend="ital">the hair.</hi> (Msb.)          <sense type="b" n="8">-b8-</sense>  <hi rend="ital">He,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">it, took by force;</hi> or <hi rend="ital">seized:</hi> (B:) <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  <hi rend="ital">he,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">it, overcame, overpowered,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">subdued:</hi> said by some to be the primary signification. (MF.) [See also <foreign lang="ar">أَخَذَهُ عَلْوَّا</foreign>, &amp;c., in art. <foreign lang="ar">علو</foreign>: and <foreign lang="ar">أَخَذَهُ مِنْ فَوْقُ</foreign>, &amp;c., in art. <foreign lang="ar">فوق</foreign>.] It is said in the Kur [ii. 256], <foreign lang="ar">لَا تَأْخُذُهُ سِنَةِ وَ لَا نَوْمٌ</foreign> <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  <hi rend="ital">Neither drowsiness nor sleep shall seize</hi> [or <hi rend="ital">overcome</hi>] <hi rend="ital">Him.</hi> (B.) [And you say, <foreign lang="ar">أَخَذَتْهُ رِعْدَةٌ</foreign> <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  <hi rend="ital">A tremour seized, took, affected,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">influenced, him.</hi> And <foreign lang="ar">أَخَذَهُ بَطْنُهُ</foreign> <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  <hi rend="ital">His belly affected him with a desire to evacuate it.</hi>] You say also, <foreign lang="ar">أَخَذَ فِيهِ الشَّرَابُ</foreign> <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  <hi rend="ital">The wine affected him,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">influenced him, so that he became intoxicated.</hi> (TA in art. <foreign lang="ar">ثمل</foreign>.) And <foreign lang="ar">أَخَذَ الرَّأْسَ</foreign> (Msb in art. <foreign lang="ar">سور</foreign>, &amp;c.) and <foreign lang="ar">أَخَذَ بِالرَّأْسِ</foreign> (K in art. <foreign lang="ar">حمى</foreign>, &amp;c.) <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  [<hi rend="ital">It had an overpowering influence upon the head</hi>]; meaning wine. (Msb, K.) And <foreign lang="ar">أَخَذَ بِالحَلْقِ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">It</hi> (food, &amp;c.) <hi rend="ital">choked</hi>]. (IAar in art. <foreign lang="ar">نشب</foreign> in the TA, and S in art. <foreign lang="ar">بشع</foreign>, &amp;c.) And <foreign lang="ar">لَا يَأْخُذُ فِيهِ قَوْلُ قَائِلٍ</foreign> <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  [<hi rend="ital">Nothing that any one may say will have any power,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">effect,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">influence, upon him</hi>]; meaning that he obeyeth no one. (L in art. <foreign lang="ar">ليت</foreign>.)          <sense type="b" n="9">-b9-</sense>  <hi rend="ital">He took captive.</hi> (L, Msb, B.)                   <form>       
                     <itype>8</itype>        
                     <orth orig="" extent="full" lang="ar">ائتخذ</orth>
                     <orth extent="full" lang="ar">ذ</orth>
                  </form> [written with the disjunctive alif <foreign lang="ar">اِيتَخَذَ</foreign>] occurs in its original form; and is changed into <foreign lang="ar">ٱتَّخَذَ</foreign> [with the disjunctive alif <foreign lang="ar">اِتَّخَذَ</foreign>]; this being of the measure <foreign lang="ar">افتعل</foreign> from <foreign lang="ar">أَخْذُ</foreign>, the [radical] <foreign lang="ar">ء</foreign> being softened, and changed into <foreign lang="ar">ت</foreign>, and incorporated [into the augmentative <foreign lang="ar">ت</foreign>]: hence, when it had come to be much used in the form of <foreign lang="ar">افتعل</foreign> [thus changed], they imagined the [former] <foreign lang="ar">ت</foreign> to be a radical letter [unchanged], and formed from it a verb of the measure <foreign lang="ar">فَعِلَ</foreign>, aor. <foreign lang="ar">يَفْعَلُ</foreign>; saying, <foreign lang="ar">تَخِذَ</foreign>, aor. <foreign lang="ar">يَتْخَذُ</foreign>, (S, L, Msb, *) inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">تَخَذٌ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">تَخْذٌ</foreign>: (Msb:) and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n350-1" target="ٱسْتَخَذَ" n="1" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n351"/></foreign> [written with the disjunctive alif <foreign lang="ar">اِسْتَخَذَ</foreign>], of which exs. will be found below, is also used for <foreign lang="ar">اتّخذ</foreign>; one of the two <foreign lang="ar">ت</foreign>s being changed into <foreign lang="ar">س</foreign>, like as <foreign lang="ar">س</foreign> is changed into <foreign lang="ar">ت</foreign> in <foreign lang="ar">سِتٌّ</foreign> [for <foreign lang="ar">سِدْسٌ</foreign>]: or <foreign lang="ar">استخذ</foreign> may be of the measure <foreign lang="ar">استفعل</foreign> from <foreign lang="ar">تَخِذَ</foreign>; one of the two <foreign lang="ar">ت</foreign>s being suppressed; after the manner of those who say <foreign lang="ar">ظَلْتُ</foreign> for <foreign lang="ar">ظَلِلْتُ</foreign>: (S, L:) and IAth says that <foreign lang="ar">اتّخذ</foreign>, in like manner, is of the measure <foreign lang="ar">افتعل</foreign> from <foreign lang="ar">تَخِذَ</foreign>; not from <foreign lang="ar">أَخَذَ</foreign>: (L and K in art. <foreign lang="ar">تخذ</foreign>:) but IAth is not one who should contradict J, whose opinion on this point is corroborated by the fact that they say <foreign lang="ar">ٱتَّزَرَ</foreign> from <foreign lang="ar">إِزَارٌ</foreign>, and <foreign lang="ar">ٱتَّمَنَ</foreign> from <foreign lang="ar">أَمْنٌ</foreign>, and <foreign lang="ar">ٱتَّهَلَ</foreign> from <foreign lang="ar">أَهْلٌ</foreign>; and there are other instances of the same kind: or, accord. to some, <foreign lang="ar">اتّخذ</foreign> is from <foreign lang="ar">وَخَذَ</foreign>, a dial. var. of <foreign lang="ar">أَخَذَ</foreign>, and is originally <foreign lang="ar">اِوْتَخَذَ</foreign>. (MF.) [The various significations of <foreign lang="ar">اتّخذ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">تَخِذَ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">استخذ</foreign> will be here given under one head.]          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  You say, <foreign lang="ar">إِئْتَخَذُوا فِى القِتَالِ</foreign>, (S, L, K, *) and <foreign lang="ar">فى الحَرْبِ</foreign>, (Msb,) with two hemzehs, (S, L, K,) or, correctly, <foreign lang="ar">إِيتَخَذُوا</foreign>, with one hemzeh, [or <foreign lang="ar">اِيتَخَذُوا</foreign>,] as two hemzehs cannot occur together in one word, (marginal note in a copy of the S,) [but in a case of wasl, the first hemzeh being suppressed, the second remains unchanged,] <hi rend="ital">They took,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">seized,</hi> (<foreign lang="ar">أَخَذُوا</foreign>,) <hi rend="ital">one another</hi> (S, L, Msb, K) <hi rend="ital">in fight,</hi> (S, L,) and <hi rend="ital">in war;</hi> (Msb;) and so <foreign lang="ar">اِتَّخَذُوا</foreign>. (Msb.) And <foreign lang="ar">اِيتَخَذَ القَوْمُ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">The people,</hi> of <hi rend="ital">company of men, wrestled together, each taking hold in some manner upon him who wrestled with him, to throw him down.</hi> (L, TA.)          <sense type="b" n="3">-b3-</sense>  [<foreign lang="ar">اتّخذ</foreign>, as also   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n350-2" target="استخذ" n="2" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign>, and] <foreign lang="ar">تَخِذَ</foreign>, aor.      
    <form n="infl">       
                     <orth orig="Ba" lang="ar">اَخَذَ</orth>
                  </form>, (K in art. <foreign lang="ar">تخذ</foreign>,) inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">تَخَذَ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">تَخْذٌ</foreign>, (TA in art. <foreign lang="ar">تخذ</foreign>,) likewise signifies <hi rend="ital">i. q.</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">أَخَذَ</foreign>, (K in art. <foreign lang="ar">تخذ</foreign>, and B and TA in the present art.,) as meaning <hi rend="ital">He took</hi> a thing <hi rend="ital">to,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">for, himself; took possession of</hi> it; <hi rend="ital">got,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">acquired,</hi> it; syn. <foreign lang="ar">حَازَ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">حَصَّلَ</foreign>. Some read, [in the Kur, xviii. 76,] <foreign lang="ar">لَتَخِذْتَ عَلَيْهِ أَجْراً</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">Thou mightest assuredly have taken for thyself a recompense for it</hi>]: (S, L, K in art. <foreign lang="ar">تخذ</foreign>, and TA in the present art.:) this is the reading of Mujáhid, (Fr, TA,) and is authorized by I'Ab, and is that of Aboo-'Amr Ibn-El-'Alà and AZ, and so it is written in the model-copy of the Kur, and so the readers [in general] read: (AM, L, TA:) so read Ibn-Ketheer and the Basrees; he and Yaakoob and Hafs pronouncing the <foreign lang="ar">ذ</foreign>; the others incorporating it [into the <foreign lang="ar">ت</foreign>]: (Bd:) some read <foreign lang="ar">لاٱتَّخَذتَّ</foreign>; (L and K in art. <foreign lang="ar">تخذ</foreign>;) but these read at variance with the scripture. And <foreign lang="ar">تَخِذَ</foreign>, aor.      
    <form n="infl">
